Brief introductions to the debates regarding the anthropology of religion, magic, and science are provided in Graham Cunningham, [3m
Religion and Magic: Approaches and Theories [0m(Edinburgh, 1999), and Rebecca L. Stein and Philip L. Stein, [3mThe Anthropology of
